Le client web est hébergé sur **Supabase**.\n     7→La collaboration passe par **Supabase Realtime** au lieu de WebSocket custom.\n     8→\n     9→```\n    10→┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    11→│ Claude (Desktop / claude.ai)                           │\n    12→│ MCP Streamable HTTP → Edge Function                    │\n    13→└────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    14→             │\n    15→┌────────────▼───────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    16→│ Supabase Edge Function                                 │\n    17→│ packs/illustrator.ts — 36 outils DSL agent             │\n    18→│ ├── positionnement relatif (below, center_h, gap)      │\n    19→│ ├── batch operations (batch_add, batch_update)         │\n    20→│ ├── layout analysis (check_layout)                     │\n    21→│ ├── text measurement (opentype.js)                     │\n    22→│ └── exports (SVG, PNG, DOCX)                           │\n    23→├────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    24→│            │ SQL (postgres.js)                          │\n    25→│ PostgreSQL │                                           │\n    26→│ ├── cad.drawing (document canvas)                      │\n    27→│ ├── cad.shape (éléments: text, image, rect, line)      │\n    28→│ ├── cad.layer (calques)                                │\n    29→│ ├── illustrator.asset (métadonnées images)             │\n    30→│ └── cad.render_svg() (rendu serveur)                   │\n    31→├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    32→│ Realtime   │ Postgres Changes → push au client         │\n    33→│            │ Broadcast → toasts, selection sync         │\n    34→├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    35→│ Storage    │ Bucket \"assets\" (images utilisateur)       │\n    36→│            │ Bucket \"exports\" (PDF, SVG, DOCX temp)     │\n    37→├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    38→│ Auth       │ OAuth 2.0 (Claude Directory)              │\n    39→└────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    40→             │\n    41→┌────────────▼───────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    42→│ Client Web (Supabase static / Vercel)                  │\n    43→│ ├── D3 SVG canvas (drag, snap, selection)              │\n    44→│ ├── Image editor modal (crop, filters)                 │\n    45→│ ├── Asset library panel (photothèque)                  │\n    46→│ ├── Undo/redo manager                                  │\n    47→│ ├── State machine (phases: idle → selected → dragging) │\n    48→│ └── supabase-js (Realtime subscribe + Storage URLs)    │\n    49→└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    50→```\n    51→\n    52→## Les 5 piliers à préserver\n    53→\n    54→### 1. Collaboration bidirectionnelle\n    55→\n    56→**Aujourd'hui** : WebSocket custom + `requestFromClient()` (request/response over WS).\n    57→Claude envoie un message typé au client, le client répond avec `_reqId`.\n    58→\n    59→**Cible** : Supabase Realtime (Broadcast channel).\n    60→- Canal `doc-{drawingId}` : Postgres Changes sur cad.drawing + cad.shape\n    61→- Canal `collab-{drawingId}` : Broadcast pour selection sync, toasts, inspect\n    62→\n    63→**Équivalences** :\n    64→\n    65→| Aujourd'hui (WS) | Cible (Realtime) |\n    66→|-------------------|------------------|\n    67→| `{ type: \"state\", doc, docList }` | Postgres Changes sur drawing/shape |\n    68→| `{ type: \"select_element\", id }` | Broadcast `{ event: \"select\", elementId }` |\n    69→| `{ type: \"select_asset\", path }` | Broadcast `{ event: \"select_asset\", path }` |\n    70→| `{ type: \"toast\", text, level }` | Broadcast `{ event: \"toast\", text, level }` |\n    71→| `requestFromClient(\"inspect\")` | Broadcast request + response pattern |\n    72→| `requestFromClient(\"dispatch\")` | Broadcast `{ event: \"dispatch\", payload }` |\n    73→| `{ type: \"reload\" }` | N/A (pas de hot reload en prod) |\n    74→\n    75→### 2. Éditeur complet standalone\n    76→\n    77→Le client D3/SVG reste quasi-identique. Changements :\n    78→- **WS → supabase-js Realtime** : remplacer `ws.send()` par `channel.send()`\n    79→- **State sync** : le client écoute Postgres Changes au lieu de `{ type: \"state\" }`\n    80→- **Mutations** : le client appelle PostgREST (`/rpc/add_shape`, `/rpc/move_shape`) au lieu de WS\n    81→- **Assets** : `fetch(\"/api/assets\")` → `supabase.storage.from(\"assets\").list()`\n    82→\n    83→### 3. Asset management intelligent\n    84→\n    85→**Principe fondamental** : les images (blobs) ne transitent **jamais** par le MCP.\n    86→Le MCP ne manipule que des IDs, URLs signées, et métadonnées texte (~100-500 bytes/appel).\n    87→\n    88→**Aujourd'hui** : `assets/` filesystem + `metadata.json` statique.\n    89→\n    90→**Cible** : Supabase Storage (blobs) + table PG (métadonnées) + classification par Claude (vision).\n    91→\n    92→#### Flux upload & classification\n    93→\n    94→```\n    95→1. UPLOAD (client web → Supabase, sans MCP)\n    96→   Client web → Supabase Storage (upload direct, signed URL)\n    97→   Client web → INSERT illustrator.asset (filename, path, status: 'to_classify')\n    98→   L'image lourde ne passe que entre le navigateur et Storage.\n    99→\n   100→2. CLASSIFICATION (Claude via MCP, texte léger uniquement)\n   101→   Claude → list_assets status:'to_classify'          (~100 bytes/asset)\n   102→   Claude → get_asset_url id:123                       → URL signée (~200 bytes)\n   103→   Claude → [vision multimodale] regarde l'image via l'URL\n   104→   Claude → classify_asset id:123                      (~500 bytes)\n   105→            tags:['jazz','concert'] description:'Saxophoniste sur scène'\n   106→            width:1920 height:1080 orientation:'paysage'\n   107→\n   108→3. UTILISATION (Claude via MCP, référence par ID)\n   109→   Claude → add_image asset_id:123 below:title center_h\n   110→   PG stocke la référence (asset_id FK), pas le blob.\n   111→   Le client web charge l'image depuis Storage via URL signée.\n   112→\n   113→4. BROWSE (client web, sans MCP)\n   114→   Client web → SELECT * FROM illustrator.asset WHERE user_id = $1\n   115→   Client web → Supabase Storage thumbnails (Image Transformation API)\n   116→   L'utilisateur browse, sélectionne → état sync via Realtime → Claude le voit.\n   117→```\n   118→\n   119→#### Outils MCP asset\n   120→\n   121→| Outil | Input | Output | Taille |\n   122→|-------|-------|--------|--------|\n   123→| `list_assets` | status, tags[], q (FTS) | id, filename, tags, description, dimensions | ~100 bytes/asset |\n   124→| `get_asset_url` | asset_id | URL signée temporaire (60min) | ~200 bytes |\n   125→| `classify_asset` | asset_id, tags, description, etc. | confirmation | ~100 bytes |\n   126→| `delete_asset` | asset_id | confirmation | ~50 bytes |\n   127→\n   128→**Zéro blob dans le contexte MCP. Jamais.**\n   129→\n   130→#### Schéma PG\n   131→\n   132→```sql\n   133→CREATE TABLE illustrator.asset (\n   134→  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n   135→  user_id     UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n   136→  path        TEXT NOT NULL,              -- Storage bucket path\n   137→  filename    TEXT NOT NULL,\n   138→  mime_type   TEXT NOT NULL,\n   139→  status      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'to_classify'\n   140→              CHECK (status IN ('to_classify', 'classified', 'archived')),\n   141→  -- Dimensions (remplies à l'upload par le client ou à la classification)\n   142→  width       INTEGER,\n   143→  height      INTEGER,\n   144→  orientation TEXT,                        -- portrait/paysage\n   145→  -- Métadonnées (remplies par Claude via classify_asset)\n   146→  title       TEXT,\n   147→  description TEXT,\n   148→  tags        TEXT[],\n   149→  credit      TEXT,\n   150→  saison      TEXT,                        -- printemps/été/automne/hiver\n   151→  usage_hint  TEXT,                        -- affiche, tract, bulletin, web\n   152→  colors      TEXT[],                      -- couleurs dominantes extraites\n   153→  -- Timestamps\n   154→  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),\n   155→  classified_at TIMESTAMPTZ\n   156→);\n   157→\n   158→-- RLS\n   159→ALTER TABLE illustrator.asset ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\n   160→CREATE POLICY \"Users see own assets\" ON illustrator.asset\n   161→  FOR ALL USING (auth.uid() = user_id);\n   162→\n   163→-- FTS sur description + tags\n   164→ALTER TABLE illustrator.asset ADD COLUMN search_vec tsvector\n   165→  GENERATED ALWAYS AS (\n   166→    setweight(to_tsvector('pgv_search', coalesce(title,'')), 'A') ||\n   167→    setweight(to_tsvector('pgv_search', coalesce(description,'')), 'B') ||\n   168→    setweight(to_tsvector('pgv_search', coalesce(array_to_string(tags,' '),'')), 'A')\n   169→  ) STORED;\n   170→CREATE INDEX idx_asset_search ON illustrator.asset USING GIN(search_vec);\n   171→CREATE INDEX idx_asset_user ON illustrator.asset(user_id);\n   172→CREATE INDEX idx_asset_status ON illustrator.asset(user_id, status);\n   173→CREATE INDEX idx_asset_tags ON illustrator.asset USING GIN(tags);\n   174→```\n   175→\n   176→#### L'utilisateur Claude Desktop\n   177→\n   178→L'utilisateur dans Claude Desktop peut aussi fournir des images directement dans le chat :\n   179→- Claude reçoit l'image en base64 dans le message (géré par Claude Desktop, pas par le MCP)\n   180→- Claude appelle un outil `upload_from_chat` qui prend le base64, le push dans Storage + crée l'entrée PG\n   181→- Exception : c'est le seul cas où un blob transite via le MCP, mais c'est Claude Desktop qui le gère nativement\n   182→\n   183→```\n   184→Utilisateur : \"Voici le logo\" [upload image dans Claude Desktop]\n   185→Claude : → upload_from_chat(base64, filename:\"logo.png\")\n   186→         → classify_asset(tags:['logo','festival'], ...)\n   187→         → add_image(asset_id:456, center_h:true, y:20)\n   188→```\n   189→\n   190→### 4. DSL agent (pack illustrator.ts)\n   191→\n   192→Le pack TypeScript porte la logique métier qui ne peut pas être en PG :\n   193→- `positioning.ts` — positionnement relatif (below, right_of, center_h, gap)\n   194→- `fonts.ts` — mesure texte (opentype.js, pas de WASM en PG)\n   195→- `layout.ts` — check_layout (overlaps, bleed, spacing, color warnings)\n   196→- `tree.ts` — traversée arbre éléments\n   197→- Exports : SVG (peut être en PG via cad.render_svg), PNG (resvg), DOCX (npm:docx)\n   198→\n   199→Mapping outils → implémentation :\n   200→\n   201→| Outil | Logique | Stockage |\n   202→|-------|---------|----------|\n   203→| `doc_new` | Pack: format/orientation defaults | PG: `INSERT INTO cad.drawing` |\n   204→| `add_text` | Pack: positioning + font measure | PG: `cad.add_shape(type:'text', props)` |\n   205→| `add_image` | Pack: positioning + dimensions | PG: `cad.add_shape(type:'image', props)` + Storage |\n   206→| `update_element` | Pack: validate props | PG: `UPDATE cad.shape SET props = ...` |\n   207→| `align` / `distribute` | Pack: compute deltas | PG: batch `UPDATE cad.shape` |\n   208→| `get_state` | Pack: compact format | PG: `SELECT * FROM cad.shape WHERE drawing_id = $1` |\n   209→| `check_layout` | Pack: analyse complète | PG: read shapes |\n   210→| `measure_text` | Pack: opentype.js | Aucun |\n   211→| `snapshot` | Pack: resvg | PG: `cad.render_svg()` |\n   212→| `export_svg` | PG ou Pack | PG: `cad.render_svg()` |\n   213→| `list_assets` | PG | PG: `SELECT * FROM illustrator.asset` |\n   214→| `inspect_store` | Realtime | Broadcast request/response |\n   215→| `show_message` | Realtime | Broadcast toast |\n   216→\n   217→### 5. Export pipeline\n   218→\n   219→| Format | Aujourd'hui | Cible |\n   220→|--------|------------|-------|\n   221→| SVG | `buildSVG()` TS | `cad.render_svg()` PG (enrichi pour illustrator) |\n   222→| PNG | resvg (Bun native) | resvg (npm:@resvg/resvg-js) — à tester en Edge |\n   223→| PDF | Puppeteer headless | pdf-lib pur (pas de Chrome) ou service externe |\n   224→| DOCX | npm:docx | npm:docx (compatible Deno) |\n   225→\n   226→## Phases de migration\n   227→\n   228→### Phase 0 — Préparation CAD 2D (1-2j)\n   229→- Étendre `cad.shape.props` pour supporter les propriétés illustrator `doc_save`, `doc_delete`, `add_text`, `add_rect`, `add_image`, `update_element`, `get_state`\n   238→- Monter dans l'Edge Function + tester via Claude Desktop\n   239→\n   240→### Phase 2 — Outils {"parentUuid":"d3b09899-5775-40ba-994e-76e72166914b","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"a2c8a58b-8129-4386-ab52-e0c66d300d73","agentId":"a25dc0ced943a976f","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01WPi9cMYqgZqLuqzVtE1HYd","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# ILLUSTRATOR.md — Integration MCP Illustrator\n     2→\n     3→> Moteur de rendu documentaire pour la plateforme pgView.\n     4→> MCP Illustrator est le composant de composition et d'export PDF pour tous les documents : devis, factures, brochures produits, communication.\n     5→\n     6→## Vision\n     7→\n     8→Deux mondes, un seul moteur de rendu :\n     9→\n    10→```\n    11→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    12→|  pgView (PostgreSQL)           |  MCP Illustrator                |\n    13→|  ============================  |  ============================== |\n    14→|  Affichage web interactif      |  Documents imprimables (PDF)    |\n    15→|  get_devis() -> HTML browser   |  Composition A4 -> PDF 300 DPI  |\n    16→|  Navigation, CRUD, workflow    |  Brochures, catalogues, com'    |\n    17→|  Temps reel, Alpine.js shell   |  Export pro, bleed, crop marks  |\n    18→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    19→                  |                              |\n    20→                  +--------- bridge -------------+\n    21→                  |                              |\n    22→          Donnees metier (PL/pgSQL)     Layout (Illustrator tools)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→pgView genere le HTML pour le navigateur. Illustrator compose les documents pour l'impression et l'export. Les donnees viennent du meme endroit : PostgreSQL.\n    26→\n    27→## Pourquoi Illustrator (pas un moteur HTML-to-PDF)\n    28→\n    29→Les moteurs HTML-to-PDF (Gotenberg, WeasyPrint, Puppeteer) convertissent du HTML en PDF. Ca marche, mais :\n    30→\n    31→| | HTML-to-PDF | Illustrator |\n    32→|---|------------|-------------|\n    33→| Controle layout | CSS @page, limites navigateur | Millimetrique, pixel-perfect |\n    34→| Typographie | Approximative (navigateur) | Precise (opentype.js, mesure glyphes) |\n    35→| Images | Contraintes CSS | Crop, zoom, filtres, ombres |\n    36→| Bleed / crop marks | Hack ou impossible | Natif, configurable |\n    37→| Brochures / com' | Hors scope | Use case principal |\n    38→| Template reutilisable | HTML + CSS a maintenir | Document clonable |\n    39→| UI de design | Aucune | Editeur web interactif |\n    40→| Clients potentiels | Aucun (c'est de l'infra) | Produit vendable separement |\n    41→\n    42→L'argument decisif : Illustrator sert **aussi** pour la communication (brochures, flyers, catalogues produit). Un moteur HTML-to-PDF ne fait que de la conversion — Illustrator est un outil de creation.\n    43→\n    44→## Architecture d'integration\n    45→\n    46→### Composants\n    47→\n    48→```\n    49→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    50→|  plpgsql-workbench        |        |  mcp-illustrator          |\n    51→|  (MCP server :3100)       |        |  (MCP server, stdio)      |\n    52→|                           |        |                           |\n    53→|  pg_query / pg_get        |        |  doc_new / doc_duplicate  |\n    54→|  -> donnees metier        |        |  batch_add / batch_update |\n    55→|                           |        |  export_pdf / snapshot    |\n    56→|  quote.devis_data(id)     |        |                           |\n    57→|  quote.facture_data(id)   |        |  Templates = documents    |\n    58→|  crm.client_data(id)      |        |  stockes dans SQLite      |\n    59→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    60→              |                                    |\n    61→              +------------- bridge ---------------+\n    62→              |                                    |\n    63→     +------------------+                          |\n    64→     |  Orchestrateur   |  (agent Claude, MCP tool, ou script)\n    65→     |  1. Query data   |\n    66→     |  2. Clone template|\n    67→     |  3. Fill data     |\n    68→     |  4. Export PDF    |\n    69→     +------------------+\n    70→```\n    71→\n    72→### Flux de generation\n    73→\n    74→```\n    75→1. QUERY     pg_query(\"SELECT quote.devis_data(42)\")\n    76→             -> { numero, date, client, lignes[], totaux, mentions[] }\n    77→\n    78→2. CLONE     doc_duplicate(\"tpl-devis-standard\")\n    79→             -> nouveau document \"DEV-2026-042\"\n    80→\n    81→3. FILL      batch_update([\n    82→               { name: \"numero\",     text: \"DEV-2026-042\" },\n    83→               { name: \"date\",       text: \"13 mars 2026\" },\n    84→               { name: \"client-nom\", text: \"Dupont SARL\" },\n    85→               ...\n    86→             ])\n    87→             + generation dynamique du tableau de lignes\n    88→\n    89→4. EXPORT    export_pdf({ format: \"A4\", home_print: true })\n    90→             -> PDF binaire\n    91→\n    92→5. CLEANUP   doc_delete(\"DEV-2026-042\")\n    93→             (ou archivage si besoin de re-generation)\n    94→```\n    95→\n    96→## Templates\n    97→\n    98→### Principe : template = document\n    99→\n   100→Pas de DSL, pas de Jinja, pas de moteur de substitution. Un template est un **document Illustrator standard** avec des elements nommes :\n   101→\n   102→```\n   103→tpl-devis-standard (A4 portrait)\n   104→├── logo              image    (x:15, y:15, w:40, h:20)\n   105→├── entreprise-nom    text     (x:15, y:40, \"ACME SARL\")\n   106→├── entreprise-addr   text     (x:15, y:48, \"12 rue des Lilas...\")\n   107→├── entreprise-siret  text     (x:15, y:62, \"SIRET: 123 456 789 00001\")\n   108→├── entreprise-tva    text     (x:15, y:67, \"TVA: FR12345678900\")\n   109→├── client-nom        text     (x:120, y:40, \"[client]\")\n   110→├── client-addr       text     (x:120, y:48, \"[adresse]\")\n   111→├── titre             text     (x:15, y:90, \"DEVIS DEV-XXXX-XXX\")\n   112→├── date              text     (x:160, y:90, \"[date]\")\n   113→├── validite          text     (x:160, y:96, \"Valide 30 jours\")\n   114→├── table-header      group    (y:110)\n   115→│   ├── col-desc      text     \"Description\"\n   116→│   ├── col-qte       text     \"Qte\"\n   117→│   ├── col-unite     text     \"Unite\"\n   118→│   ├── col-pu        text     \"P.U. HT\"\n   119→│   ├── col-tva       text     \"TVA\"\n   120→│   └── col-total     text     \"Total HT\"\n   121→├── table-lines       group    (y:118, genere dynamiquement)\n   122→├── total-ht          text     (x:160, y: calc, \"Total HT: 1 234,00\")\n   123→├── total-tva         text     (x:160, y: calc, \"TVA 20%:   246,80\")\n   124→├── total-ttc         text     (x:160, y: calc, \"Total TTC: 1 480,80\")\n   125→├── mentions          group    (y: bottom - 40)\n   126→│   ├── mention-1     text     \"Delai de paiement: 30 jours...\"\n   127→│   ├── mention-2     text     \"Penalites de retard: 10%...\"\n   128→│   └── mention-3     text     \"Indemnite forfaitaire: 40 EUR\"\n   129→├── watermark         text     (center, rotate:-45, opacity:0.08, \"BROUILLON\")\n   130→└── footer            group    (y: bottom - 10)\n   131→    ├── page-num      text     \"Page 1/1\"\n   132→    └── generation    text     \"Genere le 13/03/2026\"\n   133→```\n   134→\n   135→### Convention de nommage\n   136→\n   137→Les elements portent des noms semantiques que l'orchestrateur connait :\n   138→\n   139→| Prefixe | Contenu | Source |\n   140→|---------|---------|--------|\n   141→| `entreprise-*` | Coordonnees emetteur | `workbench.config('quote', ...)` |\n   142→| `client-*` | Coordonnees destinataire | `crm.client` |\n   143→| `titre`, `numero`, `date` | En-tete document | `quote.devis` / `quote.facture` |\n   144→| `table-header`, `table-lines` | Tableau des lignes | `quote.ligne` |\n   145→| `total-*` | Bloc totaux | Calcul `_total_ht/tva/ttc` |\n   146→| `mention-*` | Mentions legales | `quote.mention` |\n   147→| `watermark` | Filigrane conditionnel | Statut (BROUILLON, PAYE, ANNULE) |\n   148→| `footer` | Pied de page | Metadata generation |\n   149→\n   150→### Types de templates\n   151→\n   152→| Template | Format | Usage |\n   153→|----------|--------|-------|\n   154→| `tpl-devis-standard` | A4 portrait | Devis classique |\n   155→| `tpl-facture-standard` | A4 portrait | Facture |\n   156→| `tpl-bon-livraison` | A4 portrait | Bon de livraison |\n   157→| `tpl-avoir` | A4 portrait | Avoir / credit |\n   158→| `tpl-relance` | A4 portrait | Lettre de relance |\n   159→| `tpl-brochure-produit` | A4 paysage | Fiche produit catalogue |\n   160→| `tpl-catalogue-*` | A3/A4 | Catalogue multi-pages |\n   161→\n   162→### Personnalisation par tenant\n   163→\n   164→Les templates sont des documents Illustrator. Personnaliser = modifier le document :\n   165→\n   166→1. **Branding** — Remplacer le logo, les couleurs, les polices\n   167→2. **Layout** — Deplacer les blocs, redimensionner\n   168→3. **Contenu fixe** — Modifier les mentions, ajouter un slogan\n   169→4. **Nouveau template** — Dupliquer + modifier via l'UI web (localhost:3333)\n   170→\n   171→Pas de systeme de \"theme\" abstrait. Le template EST le design final — l'utilisateur ou l'agent le modifie directement.\n   172→\n   173→## Donnees metier\n   174→\n   175→### Fonctions d'extraction\n   176→\n   177→Chaque module expose une fonction `*_data()` qui retourne un JSONB structure, pret pour le remplissage :\n   178→\n   179→```sql\n   180→-- quote.devis_data(p_id int) RETURNS jsonb\n   181→{\n   182→  \"numero\": \"DEV-2026-042\",\n   183→  \"date\": \"2026-03-13\",\n   184→  \"validite\": \"2026-04-12\",\n   185→  \"statut\": \"brouillon\",\n   186→\n   187→  \"entreprise\": {\n   188→    \"nom\": \"ACME SARL\",\n   189→    \"adresse\": \"12 rue des Lilas, 39000 Lons-le-Saunier\",\n   190→    \"siret\": \"123 456 789 00001\",\n   191→    \"tva_intra\": \"FR12345678900\",\n   192→    \"telephone\": \"03 84 XX XX XX\",\n   193→    \"email\": \"contact@acme.fr\"\n   194→  },\n   195→\n   196→  \"client\": {\n   197→    \"nom\": \"Dupont SARL\",\n   198→    \"adresse\": \"5 avenue de la Gare, 25000 Besancon\",\n   199→    \"siret\": \"987 654 321 00001\"\n   200→  },\n   201→\n   202→  \"lignes\": [\n   203→    {\n   204→      \"description\": \"Conduit inox double paroi DN150\",\n   205→      \"quantite\": 6,\n   206→      \"unite\": \"ml\",\n   207→      \"prix_unitaire\": 89.50,\n   208→      \"tva_rate\": 20,\n   209→      \"total_ht\": 537.00\n   210→    },\n   211→    ...\n   212→  ],\n   213→\n   214→  \"totaux\": {\n   215→    \"total_ht\": 1234.00,\n   216→    \"total_tva\": 246.80,\n   217→    \"total_ttc\": 1480.80,\n   218→    \"tva_detail\": [\n   219→      { \"taux\": 20, \"base\": 1234.00, \"montant\": 246.80 }\n   220→    ]\n   221→  },\n   222→\n   223→  \"mentions\": [\n   224→    { \"label\": \"Delai de paiement\", \"texte\": \"30 jours a compter de...\" },\n   225→    { \"label\": \"Penalites de retard\", \"texte\": \"10% annuel...\" },\n   226→    { \"label\": \"Indemnite forfaitaire\", \"texte\": \"40 EUR...\" }\n   227→  ]\n   228→}\n   229→```\n   230→\n   231→### Coordonnees entreprise\n   232→\n   233→Stockees dans `workbench.config` (pas dans le template) :\n   234→\n   235→```sql\n   236→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_nom');\n   237→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_siret');\n   238→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_logo_path');\n   239→-- etc.\n   240→```\n   241→\n   242→Le template contient des placeholders. L'orchestrateur les remplace par les valeurs config au moment de la generation.\n   243→\n   244→## Generation dynamique du tableau\n   245→\n   246→Le tableau de lignes est le seul element qui varie en taille. L'orchestrateur doit :\n   247→\n   248→1. **Supprimer** le groupe `table-lines` du template (placeholder)\n   249→2. **Calculer** la position Y de depart (sous `table-header`)\n   250→3. **Ajouter** une ligne par element de `lignes[]` via `batch_add`\n   251→4. **Ajuster** les positions des blocs suivants (`total-*`, `mentions`, `footer`)\n   252→\n   253→```\n   254→Pour chaque ligne:\n   255→  add_text(name: \"line-N-desc\",  x: 15,  y: Y, text: ligne.description, fontSize: 8)\n   256→  add_text(name: \"line-N-qte\",  x: 120, y: Y, text: ligne.quantite,    fontSize: 8)\n   257→  add_text(name: \"line-N-pu\",   x: 145, y: Y, text: ligne.prix_unitaire, fontSize: 8)\n   258→  add_text(name: \"line-N-total\",x: 175, y: Y, text: ligne.total_ht,    fontSize: 8)\n   259→  Y += line_height (environ 5mm)\n   260→```\n   261→\n   262→### Multi-page\n   263→\n   264→Si le tableau depasse la zone imprimable :\n   265→\n   266→1. Detecter le depassement (Y > page_height - footer_height)\n   267→2. Couper le tableau, ajouter \"Suite page suivante\"\n   268→3. Creer un second document (page 2) avec le reste des lignes\n   269→4. Generer les PDFs separement, concatener (ou gerer via un futur `multi_page` dans Illustrator)\n   270→\n   271→**Evolution Illustrator necessaire** : support multi-page natif (aujourd'hui 1 doc = 1 page).\n   272→\n   273→## Watermarks et statuts\n   274→\n   275→| Statut | Watermark | Opacite | Rotation |\n   276→|--------|-----------|---------|----------|\n   277→| `brouillon` | BROUILLON | 0.08 | -45 deg |\n   278→| `envoye` / `envoyee` | _(aucun)_ | — | — |\n   279→| `accepte` | ACCEPTE | 0.05 | -45 deg |\n   280→| `refuse` | REFUSE | 0.08 | -45 deg |\n   281→| `payee` | PAYE | 0.05 | -45 deg |\n   282→| `annule` | ANNULE | 0.10 | -45 deg |\n   283→\n   284→L'orchestrateur met a jour l'element `watermark` (texte, opacite) ou le supprime selon le statut.\n   285→\n   286→## Use cases\n   287→\n   288→### 1. Documents commerciaux (automatique)\n   289→\n   290→```\n   291→Utilisateur clique \"Telecharger PDF\" sur un devis\n   292→  -> post_devis_pdf(id)\n   293→  -> orchestrateur query data + clone template + fill + export\n   294→  -> PDF retourne au navigateur\n   295→```\n   296→\n   297→Entierement automatise. L'utilisateur ne voit jamais Illustrator.\n   298→\n   299→### 2. Brochure produit (semi-automatique)\n   300→\n   301→```\n   302→Agent recoit : \"Fais-moi une fiche produit pour le conduit DN150\"\n   303→  -> Query donnees catalogue (stock, prix, specs)\n   304→  -> doc_duplicate(\"tpl-brochure-produit\")\n   305→  -> Compose : photo produit, specs techniques, prix, argumentaire\n   306→  -> Ajuste le layout (positionnement, couleurs)\n   307→  -> export_pdf -> PDF\n   308→```\n   309→\n   310→L'agent utilise les MCP tools directement. L'utilisateur peut ensuite affiner via l'UI.\n   311→\n   312→### 3. Communication (creatif)\n   313→\n   314→```\n   315→Agent recoit : \"Cree une affiche pour les portes ouvertes du 15 avril\"\n   316→  -> doc_new format A3 portrait\n   317→  -> Compose librement (titre, photo, programme, logo, QR code)\n   318→  -> snapshot -> preview PNG\n   319→  -> Iterations avec l'utilisateur\n   320→  -> export_pdf -> PDF pro pour imprimeur\n   321→```\n   322→\n   323→Aucun template pre-defini. Composition libre pilotee par l'agent.\n   324→\n   325→## Factur-X (e-invoicing 2026-2027)\n   326→\n   327→La facturation electronique impose le format **Factur-X** : un PDF/A-3 avec XML CII embarque.\n   328→\n   329→### Pipeline\n   330→\n   331→```\n   332→1. export_pdf(facture)           -> PDF standard\n   333→2. quote.facture_xml_cii(id)     -> XML CII (genere par PL/pgSQL via xmlelement/xmlforest)\n   334→3. facturx_embed(pdf, xml)       -> PDF/A-3 avec XML attache\n   335→```\n   336→\n   337→L'etape 3 necessite un outil d'embedding (Python `factur-x` lib par Akretion, ou Ghostscript). Peut etre un service Docker sidecar minimaliste.\n   338→\n   339→### XML CII\n   340→\n   341→PL/pgSQL genere le XML nativement :\n   342→\n   343→```sql\n   344→SELECT xmlelement(\n   345→  name \"rsm:CrossIndustryInvoice\",\n   346→  xmlattributes('urn:un:unece:uncefact:data:standard:...' AS \"xmlns:rsm\"),\n   347→  xmlelement(name \"rsm:ExchangedDocumentContext\", ...),\n   348→  xmlelement(name \"rsm:ExchangedDocument\",\n   349→    xmlelement(name \"ram:ID\", f.numero),\n   350→    xmlelement(name \"ram:TypeCode\", '380'),\n   351→    xmlelement(name \"ram:IssueDateTime\", ...)\n   352→  ),\n   353→  ...\n   354→)\n   355→FROM quote.facture f WHERE f.id = p_id;\n   356→```\n   357→\n   358→Zero dependance externe pour la generation XML. Seul l'embedding dans le PDF necessite un outil tiers.\n   359→\n   360→## Evolutions Illustrator necessaires\n   361→\n   362→| Evolution | Priorite | Description |\n   363→|-----------|----------|-------------|\n   364→| **Multi-page** | Haute | Support natif de documents multi-pages (factures longues, catalogues) |\n   365→| **Tableaux** | Haute | Element `table` natif avec colonnes, lignes, auto-layout |\n   366→| **Variables** | Moyenne | Systeme `{{nom}}` optionnel pour pre-remplissage sans batch_update |\n   367→| **QR Code** | Moyenne | Generation QR natif (paiement, lien web, Factur-X) |\n   368→| **PDF/A** | Moyenne | Export PDF/A-3 natif (pre-requis Factur-X sans outil tiers) |\n   369→| **Fusion PDF** | Basse | Concatenation multi-pages en un seul fichier |\n   370→| **Styles** | Basse | Presets de styles reutilisables (police + taille + couleur = \"body\") |\n   371→\n   372→## Positionnement commercial\n   373→\n   374→```\n   375→+-----------------------------------------------+\n   376→|  Produit                | Cible               |\n   377→|======================== |=====================|\n   378→|  ERP pgView             | TPE/PME (gestion)   |\n   379→|  + Illustrator integre  | Documents pro       |\n   380→|  Illustrator standalone | Agences, artisans   |\n   381→|                         | (com', brochures)   |\n   382→+-----------------------------------------------+\n   383→```\n   384→\n   385→Illustrator a une double vie :\n   386→\n   387→1. **Composant integre** — Le moteur PDF de l'ERP. L'utilisateur final ne le voit pas, il clique \"Telecharger PDF\" et ca marche.\n   388→2. **Produit autonome** — Un outil de creation documentaire pilote par IA. Les clients l'achetent pour faire leurs brochures, flyers, catalogues.\n   389→\n   390→Cette dualite est un avantage strategique : le meme code sert deux marches.\n   391→"}]},"uuid":"ec6d40c6-3047-4b73-853b-0706a4d61d7d","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:12:16.771Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"d3b09899-5775-40ba-994e-76e72166914b","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

Illustrator compose les documents pour l'impression et l'export. Les donnees viennent du meme endroit : PostgreSQL.\\n    26→\\n    27→## Pourquoi Illustrator (pas un moteur HTML-to-PDF)\\n    28→\\n    29→Les moteurs HTML-to-PDF (Gotenberg, WeasyPrint, Puppeteer) convertissent du HTML en PDF. Ca marche, mais :\\n    30→\\n    31→| | HTML-to-PDF | Illustrator |\\n    32→|---|------------|-------------|\\n    33→| Controle layout | CSS @page, limites navigateur | Millimetrique, pixel-perfect |\\n    34→| Typographie | Approximative (navigateur) | Precise (opentype.js, mesure glyphes) |\\n    35→| Images | Contraintes CSS | Crop, zoom, filtres, ombres |\\n    36→| Bleed / crop marks | Hack ou impossible | Natif, configurable |\\n    37→| Brochures / com' | Hors scope | Use case principal |\\n    38→| Template reutilisable | HTML + CSS a maintenir | Document clonable |\\n    39→| UI de design | Aucune | Editeur web interactif |\\n    40→| Clients potentiels | Aucun (c'est de l'infra) | Produit vendable separement |\\n    41→\\n    42→L'argument decisif : Illustrator sert **aussi** pour la communication (brochures, flyers, catalogues produit). Un moteur HTML-to-PDF ne fait que de la conversion — Illustrator est un outil de creation.\\n    43→\\n    44→## Architecture d'integration\\n    45→\\n    46→### Composants\\n    47→\\n    48→```\\n    49→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\\n    50→|  plpgsql-workbench        |        |  mcp-illustrator          |\\n    51→|  (MCP server :3100)       |        |  (MCP server, stdio)      |\\n    52→|                           |        |                           |\\n    53→|  pg_query / pg_get        |        |  doc_new / doc_duplicate  |\\n    54→|  -> donnees metier        |        |  batch_add / batch_update |\\n    55→|                           |        |  export_pdf / snapshot    |\\n    56→|  quote.devis_data(id)     |        |                           |\\n    57→|  quote.facture_data(id)   |        |  Templates = documents    |\\n    58→|  crm.client_data(id)      |        |  stockes dans SQLite      |\\n    59→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\\n    60→              |                                    |\\n    61→              +------------- bridge ---------------+\\n    62→              |                                    |\\n    63→     +------------------+                          |\\n    64→     |  Orchestrateur   |  (agent Claude, MCP tool, ou script)\\n    65→     |  1. Query data   |\\n    66→     |  2. Clone template|\\n    67→     |  3. Fill data     |\\n    68→     |  4. Export PDF    |\\n    69→     +------------------+\\n    70→```\\n    71→\\n    72→### Flux de generation\\n    73→\\n    74→```\\n    75→1. QUERY     pg_query(\\\"SELECT quote.devis_data(42)\\\")\\n    76→             -> { numero, date, client, lignes[], totaux, mentions[] }\\n    77→\\n    78→2. CLONE     doc_duplicate(\\\"tpl-devis-standard\\\")\\n    79→             -> nouveau document \\\"DEV-2026-042\\\"\\n    80→\\n    81→3. FILL      batch_update([\\n    82→               { name: \\\"numero\\\",     text: \\\"DEV-2026-042\\\" },\\n    83→               { name: \\\"date\\\",       text: \\\"13 mars 2026\\\" },\\n    84→               { name: \\\"client-nom\\\", text: \\\"Dupont SARL\\\" },\\n    85→               ...\\n    86→             ])\\n    87→             + generation dynamique du tableau de lignes\\n    88→\\n    89→4. EXPORT    export_pdf({ format: \\\"A4\\\", home_print: true })\\n    90→             -> PDF binaire\\n    91→\\n    92→5. CLEANUP   doc_delete(\\\"DEV-2026-042\\\")\\n    93→             (ou archivage si besoin de re-generation)\\n    94→```\\n    95→\\n    96→## Templates\\n    97→\\n    98→### Principe : template = document\\n    99→\\n   100→Pas de DSL, pas de Jinja, pas de moteur de substitution. Un template est un **document Illustrator standard** avec des elements nommes :\\n   101→\\n   102→```\\n   103→tpl-devis-standard (A4 portrait)\\n   104→├── logo              image    (x:15, y:15, w:40, h:20)\\n   105→├── entreprise-nom    text     (x:15, y:40, \\\"ACME SARL\\\")\\n   106→├── entreprise-addr   text     (x:15, y:48, \\\"12 rue des Lilas...\\\")\\n   107→├── entreprise-siret  text     (x:15, y:62, \\\"SIRET: 123 456 789 00001\\\")\\n   108→├── entreprise-tva    text     (x:15, y:67, \\\"TVA: FR12345678900\\\")\\n   109→├── client-nom        text     (x:120, y:40, \\\"[client]\\\")\\n   110→├── client-addr       text     (x:120, y:48, \\\"[adresse]\\\")\\n   111→├── titre             text     (x:15, y:90, \\\"DEVIS DEV-XXXX-XXX\\\")\\n   112→├── date              text     (x:160, y:90, \\\"[date]\\\")\\n   113→├── validite          text     (x:160, y:96, \\\"Valide 30 jours\\\")\\n   114→├── table-header      group    (y:110)\\n   115→│   ├── col-desc      text     \\\"Description\\\"\\n   116→│   ├── col-qte       text     \\\"Qte\\\"\\n   117→│   ├── col-unite     text     \\\"Unite\\\"\\n   118→│   ├── col-pu        text     \\\"P.U. HT\\\"\\n   119→│   ├── col-tva       text     \\\"TVA\\\"\\n   120→│   └── col-total     text     \\\"Total HT\\\"\\n   121→├── table-lines       group    (y:118, genere dynamiquement)\\n   122→├── total-ht          text     (x:160, y: calc, \\\"Total HT: 1 234,00\\\")\\n   123→├── total-tva         text     (x:160, y: calc, \\\"TVA 20%:   246,80\\\")\\n   124→├── total-ttc         text     (x:160, y: calc, \\\"Total TTC: 1 480,80\\\")\\n   125→├── mentions          group    (y: bottom - 40)\\n   126→│   ├── mention-1     text     \\\"Delai de paiement: 30 jours...\\\"\\n   127→│   ├── mention-2     text     \\\"Penalites de retard: 10%...\\\"\\n   128→│   └── mention-3     text     \\\"Indemnite forfaitaire: 40 EUR\\\"\\n   129→├── watermark         text     (center, rotate:-45, opacity:0.08, \\\"BROUILLON\\\")\\n   130→└── footer            group    (y: bottom - 10)\\n   131→    ├── page-num      text     \\\"Page 1/1\\\"\\n   132→    └── generation    text     \\\"Genere le 13/03/2026\\\"\\n   133→```\\n   134→\\n   135→### Convention de nommage\\n   136→\\n   137→Les elements portent des noms semantiques que l'orchestrateur connait :\\n   138→\\n   139→| Prefixe | Contenu | Source |\\n   140→|---------|---------|--------|\\n   141→| `entreprise-*` | Coordonnees emetteur | `workbench.config('quote', ...)` |\\n   142→| `client-*` | Coordonnees destinataire | `crm.client` |\\n   143→| `titre`, `numero`, `date` | En-tete document | `quote.devis` / `quote.facture` |\\n   144→| `table-header`, `table-lines` | Tableau des lignes | `quote.ligne` |\\n   145→| `total-*` | Bloc totaux | Calcul `_total_ht/tva/ttc` |\\n   146→| `mention-*` | Mentions legales | `quote.mention` |\\n   147→| `watermark` | Filigrane conditionnel | Statut (BROUILLON, PAYE, ANNULE) |\\n   148→| `footer` | Pied de page | Metadata generation |\\n   149→\\n   150→### Types de templates\\n   151→\\n   152→| Template | Format | Usage |\\n   153→|----------|--------|-------|\\n   154→| `tpl-devis-standard` | A4 portrait | Devis classique |\\n   155→| `tpl-facture-standard` | A4 portrait | Facture |\\n   156→| `tpl-bon-livraison` | A4 portrait | Bon de livraison |\\n   157→| `tpl-avoir` | A4 portrait | Avoir / credit |\\n   158→| `tpl-relance` | A4 portrait | Lettre de relance |\\n   159→| `tpl-brochure-produit` | A4 paysage | Fiche produit catalogue |\\n   160→| `tpl-catalogue-*` | A3/A4 | Catalogue multi-pages |\\n   161→\\n   162→### Personnalisation par tenant\\n   163→\\n   164→Les templates sont des documents Illustrator. Personnaliser = modifier le document :\\n   165→\\n   166→1. **Branding** — Remplacer le logo, les couleurs, les polices\\n   167→2. **Layout** — Deplacer les blocs, redimensionner\\n   168→3. **Contenu fixe** — Modifier les mentions, ajouter un slogan\\n   169→4. **Nouveau template** — Dupliquer + modifier via l'UI web (localhost:3333)\\n   170→\\n   171→Pas de systeme de \\\"theme\\\" abstrait. Le template EST le design final — l'utilisateur ou l'agent le modifie directement.\\n   172→\\n   173→## Donnees metier\\n   174→\\n   175→### Fonctions d'extraction\\n   176→\\n   177→Chaque module expose une fonction `*_data()` qui retourne un JSONB structure, pret pour le remplissage :\\n   178→\\n   179→```sql\\n   180→-- quote.devis_data(p_id int) RETURNS jsonb\\n   181→{\\n   182→  \\\"numero\\\": \\\"DEV-2026-042\\\",\\n   183→  \\\"date\\\": \\\"2026-03-13\\\",\\n   184→  \\\"validite\\\": \\\"2026-04-12\\\",\\n   185→  \\\"statut\\\": \\\"brouillon\\\",\\n   186→\\n   187→  \\\"entreprise\\\": {\\n   188→    \\\"nom\\\": \\\"ACME SARL\\\",\\n   189→    \\\"adresse\\\": \\\"12 rue des Lilas, 39000 Lons-le-Saunier\\\",\\n   190→    \\\"siret\\\": \\\"123 456 789 00001\\\",\\n   191→    \\\"tva_intra\\\": \\\"FR12345678900\\\",\\n   192→    \\\"telephone\\\": \\\"03 84 XX XX XX\\\",\\n   193→    \\\"email\\\": \\\"contact@acme.fr\\\"\\n   194→  },\\n   195→\\n   196→  \\\"client\\\": {\\n   197→    \\\"nom\\\": \\\"Dupont SARL\\\",\\n   198→    \\\"adresse\\\": \\\"5 avenue de la Gare, 25000 Besancon\\\",\\n   199→    \\\"siret\\\": \\\"987 654 321 00001\\\"\\n   200→  },\\n   201→\\n   202→  \\\"lignes\\\": [\\n   203→    {\\n   204→      \\\"description\\\": \\\"Conduit inox double paroi DN150\\\",\\n   205→      \\\"quantite\\\": 6,\\n   206→      \\\"unite\\\": \\\"ml\\\",\\n   207→      \\\"prix_unitaire\\\": 89.50,\\n   208→      \\\"tva_rate\\\": 20,\\n   209→      \\\"total_ht\\\": 537.00\\n   210→    },\\n   211→    ...\\n   212→  ],\\n   213→\\n   214→  \\\"totaux\\\": {\\n   215→    \\\"total_ht\\\": 1234.00,\\n   216→    \\\"total_tva\\\": 246.80,\\n   217→    \\\"total_ttc\\\": 1480.80,\\n   218→    \\\"tva_detail\\\": [\\n   219→      { \\\"taux\\\": 20, \\\"base\\\": 1234.00, \\\"montant\\\": 246.80 }\\n   220→    ]\\n   221→  },\\n   222→\\n   223→  \\\"mentions\\\": [\\n   224→    { \\\"label\\\": \\\"Delai de paiement\\\", \\\"texte\\\": \\\"30 jours a compter de...\\\" },\\n   225→    { \\\"label\\\": \\\"Penalites de retard\\\", \\\"texte\\\": \\\"10% annuel...\\\" },\\n   226→    { \\\"label\\\": \\\"Indemnite forfaitaire\\\", \\\"texte\\\": \\\"40 EUR...\\\" }\\n   227→  ]\\n   228→}\\n   229→```\\n   230→\\n   231→### Coordonnees entreprise\\n   232→\\n   233→Stockees dans `workbench.config` (pas dans le template) :\\n   234→\\n   235→```sql\\n   236→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_nom');\\n   237→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_siret');\\n   238→SELECT workbench.config('quote', 'entreprise_logo_path');\\n   239→-- etc.\\n   240→```\\n   241→\\n   242→Le template contient des placeholders. L'orchestrateur les remplace par les valeurs config au moment de la generation.\\n   243→\\n   244→## Generation dynamique du tableau\\n   245→\\n   246→Le tableau de lignes est le seul element qui varie en taille. L'orchestrateur doit :\\n   247→\\n   248→1. **Supprimer** le groupe `table-lines` du template (placeholder)\\n   249→2. **Calculer** la position Y de depart (sous `table-header`)\\n   250→3. **Ajouter** une ligne par element de `lignes[]` via `batch_add`\\n   251→4. **Ajuster** les positions des blocs suivants (`total-*`, `mentions`, `footer`)\\n   252→\\n   253→```\\n   254→Pour chaque ligne:\\n   255→  add_text(name: \\\"line-N-desc\\\",  x: 15,  y: Y, text: ligne.description, fontSize: 8)\\n   256→  add_text(name: \\\"line-N-qte\\\",  x: 120, y: Y, text: ligne.quantite,    fontSize: 8)\\n   257→  add_text(name: \\\"line-N-pu\\\",   x: 145, y: Y, text: ligne.prix_unitaire, fontSize: 8)\\n   258→  add_text(name: \\\"line-N-total\\\",x: 175, y: Y, text: ligne.total_ht,    fontSize: 8)\\n   259→  Y += line_height (environ 5mm)\\n   260→```\\n   261→\\n   262→### Multi-page\\n   263→\\n   264→Si le tableau depasse la zone imprimable :\\n   265→\\n   266→1. Detecter le depassement (Y > page_height - footer_height)\\n   267→2. Couper le tableau, ajouter \\\"Suite page suivante\\\"\\n   268→3. Creer un second document (page 2) avec le reste des lignes\\n   269→4. Generer les PDFs separement, concatener (ou gerer via un futur `multi_page` dans Illustrator)\\n   270→\\n   271→**Evolution Illustrator necessaire** : support multi-page natif (aujourd'hui 1 doc = 1 page).\\n   272→\\n   273→## Watermarks et statuts\\n   274→\\n   275→| Statut | Watermark | Opacite | Rotation |\\n   276→|--------|-----------|---------|----------|\\n   277→| `brouillon` | BROUILLON | 0.08 | -45 deg |\\n   278→| `envoye` / `envoyee` | _(aucun)_ | — | — |\\n   279→| `accepte` | ACCEPTE | 0.05 | -45 deg |\\n   280→| `refuse` | REFUSE | 0.08 | -45 deg |\\n   281→| `payee` | PAYE | 0.05 | -45 deg |\\n   282→| `annule` | ANNULE | 0.10 | -45 deg |\\n   283→\\n   284→L'orchestrateur met a jour l'element `watermark` (texte, opacite) ou le supprime selon le statut.\\n   285→\\n   286→## Use cases\\n   287→\\n   288→### 1. Documents commerciaux (automatique)\\n   289→\\n   290→```\\n   291→Utilisateur clique \\\"Telecharger PDF\\\" sur un devis\\n   292→  -> post_devis_pdf(id)\\n   293→  -> orchestrateur query data + clone template + fill + export\\n   294→  -> PDF retourne au navigateur\\n   295→```\\n   296→\\n   297→Entierement automatise. L'utilisateur ne voit jamais Illustrator.\\n   298→\\n   299→### 2. Brochure produit (semi-automatique)\\n   300→\\n   301→```\\n   302→Agent recoit : \\\"Fais-moi une fiche produit pour le conduit DN150\\\"\\n   303→  -> Query donnees catalogue (stock, prix, specs)\\n   304→  -> doc_duplicate(\\\"tpl-brochure-produit\\\")\\n   305→  -> Compose : photo produit, specs techniques, prix, argumentaire\\n   306→  -> Ajuste le layout (positionnement, couleurs)\\n   307→  -> export_pdf -> PDF\\n   308→```\\n   309→\\n   310→L'agent utilise les MCP tools directement. L'utilisateur peut ensuite affiner via l'UI.\\n   311→\\n   312→### 3. Communication (creatif)\\n   313→\\n   314→```\\n   315→Agent recoit : \\\"Cree une affiche pour les portes ouvertes du 15 avril\\\"\\n   316→  -> doc_new format A3 portrait\\n   317→  -> Compose librement (titre, photo, programme, logo, QR code)\\n   318→  -> snapshot -> preview PNG\\n   319→  -> Iterations avec l'utilisateur\\n   320→  -> export_pdf -> PDF pro pour imprimeur\\n   321→```\\n   322→\\n   323→Aucun template pre-defini. Composition libre pilotee par l'agent.\\n   324→\\n   325→## Factur-X (e-invoicing 2026-2027)\\n   326→\\n   327→La facturation electronique impose le format **Factur-X** : un PDF/A-3 avec XML CII embarque.\\n   328→\\n   329→### Pipeline\\n   330→\\n   331→```\\n   332→1. export_pdf(facture)           -> PDF standard\\n   333→2. quote.facture_xml_cii(id)     -> XML CII (genere par PL/pgSQL via xmlelement/xmlforest)\\n   334→3. facturx_embed(pdf, xml)       -> PDF/A-3 avec XML attache\\n   335→```\\n   336→\\n   337→L'etape 3 necessite un outil d'embedding (Python `factur-x` lib par Akretion, ou Ghostscript). Peut etre un service Docker sidecar minimaliste.\\n   338→\\n   339→### XML CII\\n   340→\\n   341→PL/pgSQL genere le XML nativement :\\n   342→\\n   343→```sql\\n   344→SELECT xmlelement(\\n   345→  name \\\"rsm:CrossIndustryInvoice\\\",\\n   346→  xmlattributes('urn:un:unece:uncefact:data:standard:...' AS \\\"xmlns:rsm\\\"),\\n   347→  xmlelement(name \\\"rsm:ExchangedDocumentContext\\\", ...),\\n   348→  xmlelement(name \\\"rsm:ExchangedDocument\\\",\\n   349→    xmlelement(name \\\"ram:ID\\\", f.numero),\\n   350→    xmlelement(name \\\"ram:TypeCode\\\", '380'),\\n   351→    xmlelement(name \\\"ram:IssueDateTime\\\", ...)\\n   352→  ),\\n   353→  ...\\n   354→)\\n   355→FROM quote.facture f WHERE f.id = p_id;\\n   356→```\\n   357→\\n   358→Zero dependance externe pour la generation XML. Seul l'embedding dans le PDF necessite un outil tiers.\\n   359→\\n   360→## Evolutions Illustrator necessaires\\n   361→\\n   362→| Evolution | Priorite | Description |\\n   363→|-----------|----------|-------------|\\n   364→| **Multi-page** | Haute | Support natif de documents multi-pages (factures longues, catalogues) |\\n   365→| **Tableaux** | Haute | Element `table` natif avec colonnes, lignes, auto-layout |\\n   366→| **Variables** | Moyenne | Systeme `{{nom}}` optionnel pour pre-remplissage sans batch_update |\\n   367→| **QR Code** | Moyenne | Generation QR natif (paiement, lien web, Factur-X) |\\n   368→| **PDF/A** | Moyenne | Export PDF/A-3 natif (pre-requis Factur-X sans outil tiers) |\\n   369→| **Fusion PDF** | Basse | Concatenation multi-pages en un seul fichier |\\n   370→| **Styles** | Basse | Presets de styles reutilisables (police + taille + couleur = \\\"body\\\") |\\n   371→\\n   372→## Positionnement commercial\\n   373→\\n   374→```\\n   375→+-----------------------------------------------+\\n   376→|  Produit                | Cible               |\\n   377→|======================== |=====================|\\n   378→|  ERP pgView             | TPE/PME (gestion)   |\\n   379→|  + Illustrator integre  | Documents pro       |\\n   380→|  Illustrator standalone | Agences, artisans   |\\n   381→|                         | (com', brochures)   |\\n   382→+-----------------------------------------------+\\n   383→```\\n   384→\\n   385→Illustrator a une double vie :\\n   386→\\n   387→1. **Composant integre** — Le moteur PDF de l'ERP. L'utilisateur final ne le voit pas, il clique \\\"Telecharger PDF\\\" et ca marche.\\n   388→2. **Produit autonome** — Un outil de creation documentaire pilote par IA. Les clients l'achetent pour faire leurs brochures, flyers, catalogues.\\n   389→\\n   390→Cette dualite est un avantage strategique : le meme code sert deux marches.\\n   391→\"}]},\"uuid\":\"63b42eea-29d2-4bc5-b2ed-46c078271699\",\"timestamp\":\"2026-03-13T22:01:15.153Z\",\"sourceToolAssistantUUID\":\"c6167e3b-8569-42ca-a0ca-3672045c0995\",\"userType\":\"external\",\"cwd\":\"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench\",\"sessionId\":\"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632\",\"version\":\"2.1.75\",\"gitBranch\":\"main\",\"slug\":\"quizzical-honking-yao\"}"}]},"uuid":"1b416a43-c0c2-4913-8e24-8573ce025f56","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:13:27.313Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"257aa5b7-0c8c-4a9a-9d19-a77f182bf805","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

The actual tool count is **39 tools** (not 36 — the tools array in `src/tools.ts` includes `doc_rename`, `element_duplicate`, `add_to_group`, `remove_from_group`, `ungroup`, and `canvas_setup` which were not in the original count). The migration plan in `ILLUSTRATOR-MIGRATION.md` references 36, which excludes some helpers added later.\n\n---\n\n## Module State Summary\n\n**cad** (`modules/cad/build/cad.ddl.sql`) — Active, deployed. Tables: `drawing`, `layer`, `shape`, `piece`, `piece_group`. Shape types: `line|rect|circle|arc|polyline|text|dimension|group`. Geometry stored in `shape.geometry` (JSONB) + `shape.props` (JSONB). No `image` type. No `format`/`orientation`/`background` on drawing. Primarily a 3D CAD engine with a 2D overlay.\n\n**document** (`modules/document/build/document.ddl.sql`) — Active, deployed. Tables: `company`, `template`, `document`. Template stores `canvas` (JSONB) + `layout` (JSONB array of elements). This is the closest existing structure to Illustrator's document model.\n\n**asset** (`modules/asset/build/asset.ddl.sql`) — Active, deployed. Table: `asset.asset` with full metadata schema matching the migration plan's `illustrator.asset` almost exactly (minus `user_id` — uses `tenant_id` instead).\n\n---\n\n## Tool-by-Tool Fit Analysis\n\n### Category: Document CRUD (7 tools)\n\n| Tool | Where it fits | What exists | What's missing |\n|------|--------------|-------------|----------------|\n| `doc_new` | `document.template` (template = doc) | `document.template` table with `canvas` JSONB, `format`, `orientation`. `document.document` for instances. | No PG function `document.new_template(name, format, orientation, background, category)`. Text content in `props` is unconventional — could be in `label`. |\n| `image` | NOT in CHECK constraint | `{\"x\": float, \"y\": float}` | `{\"width\": mm, \"height\": mm, \"asset_id\": uuid, \"preserveAspectRatio\": str, \"brightness\": int, \"contrast\": int, \"grayscale\": int, \"clipX\": mm, ...}` | `image` must be added to type CHECK. `asset_id` should reference `asset.asset.id` — add as dedicated column or leave in `props`. |\n| `rect` | `rect` (exists) | `{\"x\": float, \"y\": float, \"width\": float, \"height\": float}` | `{\"fill\": hex, \"stroke\": hex, \"strokeWidth\": mm, \"rx\": mm}` | Geometry convention needs clarification: does `width`/`height` go in `geometry` or `props`? Currently inconsistent with CAD usage. |\n| `line` | `line` (exists) | `{\"x1\": float, \"y1\": float, \"x2\": float, \"y2\": float}` | `{\"stroke\": hex, \"strokeWidth\": mm}` | Fits cleanly. |\n| `group` | `group` (exists) | `{}` (no geometry — bbox computed from children) | `{}` or `{\"name\": str}` | `parent_id` self-reference already handles nesting. `label` serves as group name. |\n\n---\n\n## Element Property Mapping to cad.shape\n\nThe key architectural question is whether position/size data lives in `geometry` JSONB or `props` JSONB. The existing CAD convention is ambiguous — the DDL has both columns but no documented schema per type. The illustrator pack needs a consistent contract:\n\n**Proposed convention (clarification needed from cad agent):**\n\n```\ngeometry = spatial/positional data: {x, y} or {x1,y1,x2,y2} or {x,y,width,height}\nprops    = styling/display data: fill, stroke, fontSize, opacity, rotation, filters, etc.\n```\n\nUnder this split:\n\n| Property (Illustrator) | Column | Notes |\n|------------------------|--------|-------|\n| `x`, `y` | `geometry->>'x'`, `geometry->>'y'` | All positioned types |\n| `width`, `height` | `geometry->>'width'`, `geometry->>'height'` | rect, image |\n| `x1,y1,x2,y2` | `geometry->>'x1'` etc. | line |\n| `text` (content) | `label` column | Dedicated column, not in props JSONB |\n| `fontSize`, `fontFamily`, `fontWeight`, `fontStyle` | `props` JSONB | text type |\n| `fill`, `stroke`, `strokeWidth` | `props` JSONB | rect, line, text |\n| `rx` (border radius) | `props` JSONB | rect |\n| `textAnchor`, `maxWidth` | `props` JSONB | text |\n| `opacity`, `rotation` | `props` JSONB | all types |\n| `preserveAspectRatio` | `props` JSONB | image |\n| `brightness`, `contrast`, `grayscale` | `props` JSONB | image |\n| `clipX`, `clipY`, `clipW`, `clipH` | `props` JSONB | image |\n| `cropX`, `cropY`, `cropZoom` | `props` JSONB | image (editor-side crop) |\n| `flipH`, `flipV` | `props` JSONB | image |\n| `borderWidth`, `borderColor`, `borderRadius` | `props` JSONB | image |\n| `shadowX`, `shadowY`, `shadowBlur`, `shadowColor` | `props` JSONB | image |\n| `asset_id` | dedicated column `asset_id UUID` (add to `cad.shape`) or `props->>'asset_id'` | image — FK to asset.asset recommended for query integrity |\n\n---\n\n## Positioning Primitives — Pack vs PG\n\nAll positioning logic (`below`, `above`, `right_of`, `left_of`, `gap`, `center_h`, `center_v`) lives entirely in the pack (`positioning.ts` / `resolvePosition()`). This is correct and must remain pack-side because:\n\n1. It requires reading the current document state (bounding boxes of reference elements) before computing coordinates.\n2. `bbox()` for text requires `measureTextWidth()` from opentype.js — impossible in PG.\n3. `align` and `distribute` require the same bounding box computation.\n\nPG involvement is purely execution: the pack resolves concrete `{x, y}` coordinates and calls PG with final values.\n\n**No PG changes needed for positioning logic.** The pack's `resolvePosition()`, `computeAlign()`, `computeDistribute()`, and `distributeGrid()` functions port directly to the Edge Function with no modification.\n\n---\n\n## Document Operations — document module CRUD\n\n| Operation | PG Function Needed | document.template column used | Status |\n|-----------|-------------------|-------------------------------|--------|\n| New template | `document.new_template(name, format, orientation, bg, category)` | `name`, `format`, `orientation`, `canvas->>'bg'`, missing `category` column | Missing function + missing `category` column |\n| Save / upsert layout | `document.save_layout(id, layout jsonb)` | `layout` JSONB array | Missing function. `layout` column exists. |\n| Load by name | `document.load_by_name(name) RETURNS jsonb` | All columns | Missing function |\n| List templates | `document.list_templates(category) RETURNS jsonb` | Subset of columns | Missing function. `category` column missing. |\n| Delete template | `document.delete_template(name)` | `id` | Missing function with guard |\n| Duplicate | `document.duplicate_template(source, new_name)` | Deep copy of row | Missing function |\n| Rename | `document.rename_template(old_name, new_name)` | `name` | Missing function |\n| Update meta | `document.update_meta(id, design_notes, team_notes, rating)` | Columns missing | Missing columns + function |\n| Canvas setup | `document.canvas_setup(id, format, orientation, bg)` | `canvas`, `format`, `orientation` | Missing function |\n\nThe key insight: `document.template.layout` is the exact equivalent of Illustrator's `doc.elements` array. The pack serializes/deserializes this JSONB. Elements are stored as a flat/nested JSONB array matching the Illustrator `Element[]` type structure. The pack owns the schema of this JSONB — PG treats it as opaque blob.\n\n**Drawing ID strategy**: The migration plan uses `cad.drawing` as the canvas record and `cad.shape` as elements. However, the existing `document.template` already has `canvas` + `layout` JSONB columns that mirror the Illustrator document model more directly. There is a conflict between two approaches:\n\n**Option A (migration plan)**: Use `cad.drawing` as document, `cad.shape` as elements. Keeps elements as first-class PG rows (queryable, Realtime-friendly). Requires extending cad schema.\n\n**Option B (document module)**: Use `document.template.layout` JSONB as element store. Simpler, but elements are opaque JSONB — no per-element Realtime changes, no SQL queries on individual elements.\n\n**Decision needed**: The migration plan explicitly chose Option A (cad.drawing + cad.shape). The `document.template` then becomes a higher-level concept: templates are special drawings that get cloned for document instances. This means:\n- `document.template` stores the template `drawing_id` FK to `cad.drawing`\n- `document.document` stores the instance `drawing_id` FK to `cad.drawing`\n- Elements live in `cad.shape` for Realtime granularity\n- `document.template.layout` JSONB is either removed or kept as snapshot cache\n\n---\n\n## Asset Operations — asset module\n\n| Illustrator operation | asset module function | Status |\n|----------------------|----------------------|--------|\n| `list_assets` (status, tags, q) | `asset.search(p_params jsonb)` | Fully implemented. Filter by status, tags GIN, FTS, mime. |\n| `classify_asset` (id, title, tags, ...) | `asset.classify(p_id, p_title, ...)` | Fully implemented. Updates all metadata fields + sets status='classified'. |\n| `delete_asset` | Missing | Need `asset.delete(p_id uuid) RETURNS void` |\n| `get_asset_url` (Supabase Storage) | Missing | Requires Supabase Storage SDK — pack-side. PG has the `path` column. Pack calls `supabase.storage.from('assets').createSignedUrl(path, 3600)`. |\n| `upload_from_chat` (base64 -> Storage) | Missing | Pack-side: decode base64, upload to Storage, INSERT into `asset.asset`. |\n\nThe `asset.asset` table schema already matches the migration plan's `illustrator.asset` design with one difference: uses `tenant_id TEXT` (workbench multi-tenant) instead of `user_id UUID` (Supabase auth). This is intentional for the workbench use case.\n\n---\n\n## Export Operations — PG vs Pack\n\n| Format | PG | Pack | Storage |\n|--------|-----|------|---------|\n| SVG | `cad.render_svg(drawing_id)` — needs extension for illustrator types | `src/svg.ts` buildSVG() — current implementation | `document.document.svg_content TEXT` |\n| PNG snapshot | PG generates SVG, pack converts via resvg | resvg (`@resvg/resvg-js`) — Deno/Edge compatibility TBD | Supabase Storage bucket `exports/` |\n| PDF | No PG involvement | Puppeteer today → pdf-lib for Edge | `document.document.pdf_path TEXT` |\n| DOCX | No PG involvement | npm:docx (Deno-compatible) | `document.document` — add `docx_path TEXT` |\n\nThe `cad.render_svg()` function needs the following additions for illustrator use:\n- `<image>` element with clipPath for crop (`clipX/Y/W/H`)\n- SVG filter elements for brightness/contrast/grayscale\n- `<rect>` with `rx` for border radius\n- `<filter>` feDropShadow for shadow effects\n- `<text>` with `<tspan>` elements for word-wrapped text\n- Group nesting (`<g>` transform)\n- Rotation via `transform=\"rotate(deg, cx, cy)\"`\n\n---\n\n## Collaboration — Supabase Realtime\n\n| Illustrator mechanism | Current (WS) | Target (Realtime) | What's needed |\n|----------------------|-------------|-------------------|---------------|\n| `inspect_store` | `requestFromClient(\"inspect\")` over WS | Broadcast channel `collab-{drawingId}` request/response pattern | Pack broadcasts `{event:\"inspect_request\", reqId}`, awaits response `{event:\"inspect_response\", reqId, state}`. Timeout 5s. |\n| `dispatch_event` | WS message `{type:\"dispatch_event\", ...}` | Broadcast `{event:\"dispatch\", event_type, ...}` | Client receives and dispatches to store. |\n| `get_event_log` | WS `requestFromClient(\"event_log\")` | Broadcast request/response | Same pattern as inspect_store. |\n| `show_message` | WS `{type:\"toast\", text, level}` | Broadcast `{event:\"toast\", text, level}` | Direct broadcast, no response needed. |\n| State sync (SERVER_STATE) | WS push on every mutation | Postgres Changes on `cad.drawing` + `cad.shape` | Client subscribes to Realtime Postgres Changes — eliminates need for `SERVER_STATE` WS push entirely. |\n| Selection sync | WS `{type:\"select_element\", id}` | Broadcast `{event:\"select\", elementId}` | For multi-user presence sync. |\n\n---\n\n## Canvas Formats — Storage\n\n| Format | Dimensions (mm) | Type | Storage |\n|--------|----------------|------|---------|\n| A2 | 420 x 594 | Paper | `cad.drawing.width/height` or `document.template.canvas` JSONB |\n| A3 | 297 x 420 | Paper | Same |\n| A4 | 210 x 297 | Paper | Same — default for ERP docs |\n| A5 | 148 x 210 | Paper | Same |\n| HD | 480 x 270 | Screen | Same |\n| MACBOOK | 457 x 286 | Screen | Same |\n| IPAD | 341 x 256 | Screen | Same |\n| MOBILE | 135 x 270 | Screen | Same |\n\nThe `cad.drawing` table has `width real` and `height real` with defaults 2000x1500 (CAD units). The illustrator pack overrides these with format dimensions in mm. The `FORMATS` constant in `src/types.ts` is the authoritative lookup. `document.template` has `format TEXT` and `orientation TEXT` columns — format enum needs to match the 8 values above. Current DDL has no CHECK on format values.\n\nThe `cad.drawing` needs `format TEXT` and `background TEXT` columns added (it currently only has `width`, `height`, `unit`, `scale`, `dimension`).\n\n---\n\n## Critical Gaps Summary\n\n### cad schema gaps (Phase 0 work)\n\n1. Add `image` to `cad.shape.type` CHECK constraint\n2. Add `asset_id UUID REFERENCES asset.asset(id)` column to `cad.shape` (for image type)\n3. Add `format TEXT` column to `cad.drawing` (A2/A3/A4/A5/HD/MACBOOK/IPAD/MOBILE)\n4. Add `background TEXT` column to `cad.drawing`\n5. Add `category TEXT` column to `cad.drawing` (groups doc families)\n6. Extend `cad.render_svg()` for all illustrator element types (text tspan, image clipPath, shadow filter, border radius)\n7. Add PG functions: `add_shape`, `update_shape`, `delete_shape`, `batch_add_shapes`, `batch_update_shapes`, `group_shapes`, `ungroup_shape`, `move_to_group`, `remove_from_group`, `duplicate_shape`, `reorder_shape`, `clear_drawing`, `get_drawing_state`\n\n### document schema gaps\n\n1. Add `category TEXT` column to `document.template`\n2. Add `design_notes TEXT`, `team_notes TEXT`, `rating SMALLINT` to `document.template`\n3. Add `docx_path TEXT` to `document.document`\n4. Add `drawing_id INT REFERENCES cad.drawing(id)` to both `document.template` and `document.document` (links template/instance to their cad canvas)\n5. Clarify: does `document.template.layout` JSONB remain as snapshot or get deprecated in favour of `cad.shape` rows\n6. Add `asset.delete(p_id uuid)` function\n2. `get_asset_url` — pack-side only (Supabase Storage SDK)\n3. `upload_from_chat` — pack-side only (base64 + Storage upload)\n\n### Pack-only (no PG changes needed)\n\n- Relative positioning: `resolvePosition()`, `computeAlign()`, `computeDistribute()`, `distributeGrid()`\n- Font measurement: `measureTextWidth()`, `wrapText()` (opentype.js, no PG equivalent)\n- `check_layout`: all bounding box math, overlap detection, spacing analysis\n- `snapshot`: resvg PNG conversion\n- `export_pdf`: pdf-lib\n- `export_docx`: npm:docx\n- `get_asset_url`: Supabase Storage signed URL\n- Collaboration: Supabase Realtime Broadcast channel management\n- `inspect_store`, `dispatch_event`, `get_event_log`: Broadcast request/response\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Blueprint by Phase\n\n### Phase 0 — cad schema extension (cad agent)\n\nFiles to modify:\n- `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/modules/cad/build/cad.ddl.sql` — add `image` type, `asset_id` column, `format`/`background`/`category` columns on drawing\n- PG functions via `pg_func_set` on `cad` schema: `add_shape`, `update_shape`, `delete_shape`, `batch_add_shapes`, illustrator element types\n\n### Phase 0 — document schema extension (document agent)\n\nFiles to modify:\n- `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/modules/document/build/document.ddl.sql` — add `drawing_id` FK, `category`, meta columns, `docx_path`\n- PG functions via `pg_func_set` on `document` schema: `new_template`, `load_by_name`, `list_templates`, `save_layout`, `delete_template`, `duplicate_template`, `rename_template`, `update_meta`, `canvas_setup`\n\n### Phase 0 — asset extension (asset agent)\n\n- Add `asset.delete(p_id uuid)` function via `pg_func_set`\n\n### Phase 1 — Pack (illustrator.ts in src/core/packs/)\n\nNew file: `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/src/core/packs/illustrator.ts`\n\nPort from mcp-illustrator with these substitutions:\n- `documents.ts` (SQLite in-memory) → PG via `withClient` calling `document.*` functions\n- `assets/` filesystem → `asset.search()` + Supabase Storage\n- WebSocket `broadcast()` → Supabase Realtime channel\n- `positioning.ts` → port as-is (pure TS, no deps except `layout.ts` and `fonts.ts`)\n- `fonts.ts` → port as-is (opentype.js, Deno-compatible)\n- `layout.ts` → port as-is\n- `tree.ts` → port as-is\n- `svg.ts` → keep in pack OR call `cad.render_svg()` for the base then add illustrator-specific elements\n\n### Phase 2 — Client (Supabase static)\n\nPort `client/` replacing:\n- `ws.send()` → `channel.send()` (supabase-js Realtime)\n- `fetch(\"/rpc/...\")` → `supabase.from(...)` or PostgREST calls\n- `fetch(\"/api/assets\")` → `supabase.storage.from('assets').list()`\n\n---\n\n## Key Architectural Decision\n\nThe migration plan's choice to store elements in `cad.shape` (PG rows) rather than `document.template.layout` (opaque JSONB) is the correct one because:\n\n1. Supabase Realtime Postgres Changes fires on individual row updates — enables granular UI sync without full document rebroadcast.\n2. PG queries on individual elements are possible (e.g., \"find all text elements with asset references\").\n3. `cad.shape` already has `sort_order`, `parent_id` (group nesting), `layer_id`, `tenant_id` (isolation), `created_at` — the full infrastructure is already in place.\n\nThe `document.template.layout` JSONB column should be repurposed as a **snapshot cache** (last-known state for fast load without joining shape rows) or removed entirely. The authoritative store is always `cad.shape` rows.\n\n---\n\nRelevant files for this analysis:\n\n- `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/tools.ts` — complete tool definitions (39
